                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">

                    <milestone facs="65r4" unit="folio"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.1"> athātaḥ svabhāvavipratipattiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4"> svabhāvaprasiddhānāṃ śarīraikadeśānām
                        anyathātvaṃ maraṇāya | tad yathā śuklānāṃ kṛṣṇatvaṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ
                        śuklatvaṃ | sthirāṇām mṛdutvaṃ | calānām acalatvam acalā<pb
                            n="65v"/><lb n="1"/>nāñ calatvaṃ | pṛthūnāṃ saṃkṣiptatvaṃ
                        saṃkṣiptānāṃ pṛthutvaṃ | dīrghāṇāṃ hrasvatvaṃ ca hrasvānāṃ
                        dīrghatā | apatanadharmmiṇāṃ patanam akasmāc
                        chaityoṣṇasneharaukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇṇyāni apasarppaṇa<g
                            ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="2"/>m aṅgānāṃ svebhyaḥ
                        sthānebhyaḥ śarīraikadeśānām
                        avasraṃsotkṣiptabhrā<cb/>ntapatitavimuktanirggamātigamagurulaghutvāni
                        pravālavarṇṇavyaṅgaprādurbbhāvo vākasmāt sirāṇāṃ <lb n="3"/>ca
                        darśana lalāṭe nāsāvaṃśe vā piṭakotpattir udakotpattir
                        nne<cb/>trarogam vināsrupravṛttir lalāṭe vā prabhātakāle
                        svedapravṛttiḥ | gomayacūrṇṇaprakāśasya rajaso da<lb n="4"/>rśanam
                        uttamāṅge līyanam vā kapotakaṅkagṛddhraprabhṛtīnāṃ
                        mūtra<cb/>purīṣapravṛddhir abhuñjanānāṃ stanamūlahṛdayorassu ca
                        śūlotpattayaḥ | madhye śūnatvam anteṣu pa<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"
                            /><lb n="5"/>rimlāyitvaṃ | viparyayo vā
                        naṣṭahīnavikalavihṛtasvaraṃ vā vivarṇṇapuṣpaprādurbbhāvo vā
                        dantanakhaśarīreṣu puṣpadarśanaṃ yasya cāpsu kaphaśakṛdretāṃsi
                        nimajjanti yasya <pb n="66r"/><lb n="1"/>ca dṛṣṭimaṇḍale
                        bhinnavikṛtāni rūpāṇy ālocyante snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo bhāti
                        yaś ca durbbalo bhaktadveṣātisārābhyām pīḍyate | kāsamānaś ca
                        tṛṣṇātibhūtaḥ kṣīṇaś cha<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="2"
                        />rddibhaktadeśayuktaḥ saphenarudhirodvāmī hatasvaraḥ
                        śūlābhi<cb/>hataś ca manuṣyaśūnakaracaraṇo nnadveṣī
                        srastapiṇḍakāṃsapāṇipādaḥ | yaś ca pūrvāhṇe bhu<lb n="3"/>ktam
                        aparāhṇe ścharddayaty avidagdhaṃ sāryate vā jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ
                        <cb/>sa śvāsān mriyate | vastavad vilapamāno bhūmau patati
                        srastamuṣkaḥ stabdhaśepo bhagnagrīvaḥ praṇa<lb n="4"/>ṣṭamehaś ca
                        manuṣyaḥ prāgviśuṣyamāṇahṛdaya ārddraśarīraḥ | <cb/>yaś ca loṣṭaṃ
                        loṣṭenābhihanti | kāṣṭham vā kāṣṭhena tṛṇāni vā cchinnanti |
                        adharoṣṭham vā daśati utta<lb n="5"/>roṣṭham vā leḍhi | āluñcati
                        karṇṇau keśām̐ś ca | devadvijaguru<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"
                        />suhṛdvaidyān vā vidveṣṭi yasya ca vakrānuvakragā grahā
                        garhitasthānagatāḥ | janmaṛkṣam vāsyolkāśa<lb n="6"/>nibhyām
                        abhihanyate | rātrau vā
                        gṛhadvāraśayanāśanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbbhāvo
                        veti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5">
                        <abbr type="suspension">bha</abbr>
                        <expan>bha<ex cert="medium">vanti cātra</ex></expan> || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5ab"> cikitsyamānaḥ samyak tu vikāro <pb n="66v"
                            /><lb n="1"/>yo bhivarddhate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5cd"> prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya lakṣaṇan tadgatāyuṣaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6ab"> nivarttate mahāvyādhiḥ sahasā yasya dehinaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6cd"> na cāhāraphalaṃ yasya dṛśyate sa vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7ab"> etāni riṣṭarūpāṇi<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/>
                        <lb n="2"/>samyag budhyeta yo bhiṣak | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7cd"> sādhyāsādhyaparīkṣañ ca sa rājñaḥ
                        sa<cb/>mmato bhaved iti || 31 || ❈ || </l>

                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <milestone facs="166r  line  2" unit="folio"/>

                    <!--166r, line 2, column 2-->

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.1"> athāto vāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.2"> upadravais tu ye juṣṭā-<lb n="3"/>vyādhayo
                        yānty avāryatāṃ | rasāyanair vvinā vatsa tāṃ śṛṇv ekamanā <cb
                            n="2"/>mama || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.4"> vātavyādhiḥ pramehaś ca kuṣṭhānyatha
                        bhagandaraṃ | arśośmarī mūḍhagarbho bhavaty udaram aṣṭamam <lb
                            n="4"/>|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.5"> aṣṭāv ete mahāntaḥ syūr vvyādhayo dustarāḥ sadā
                        | prāṇamāṃsakṣa<cb n="2"/>yaḥ śophas tṛṣṇā ccharddir jvaras tathā
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.6"> atīsāraś ca mūrcchā ca
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkāśvāsas tathaiva ca | etair upa<lb n="5"/>dravair jjuṣṭān
                        sarvvān etān vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.7"> śūnaṃ suptatvacam bhagnaṅ ka<cb n="2"
                        />mpādhmānanipīḍitaṃ | rujārttam antañ ca naram vātavyādhir
                        vvināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.8"> yathoktopadravāvi<lb n="6"/>ṣṭam atiprasrutam
                        eva ca | piṭakāpīḍitaṃ gāḍhaṃ prameho hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.9"> prabhinnaṃ prasrutāṅgañ ca raktanetraṃ
                        hatasvaraṃ | pañcakarmmaguṇātītaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hanti hi kuṣṭhi<pb
                            n="66v"/>naṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.11"> vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi krimayaḥ śukram eva ca |
                        bhagandarāt prasravanti sa naśyati bhagandarī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.10">
                        <!--the manuscript switches the vulgate 's 10 and 11, as well as 13 and 14-->
                            tṛṣṇarocakaśūlārtta<lb n="2"/>m atiprasrutaśoṇitaṃ |
                        śophātīsārasaṃyuktaṃ durnāmā kṣapayen na<cb n="2"/>raṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.12"> praśūnanābhivṛṣaṇaṃ vaddhamūtrarujāturaṃ |
                        aśmarī kṣapayaty āśu sikatāśarkkarānvitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.14"> pā<lb n="3"/>rśvabhaṅgānnavidveṣaḥ
                        śophātīsārapīḍitam | vivarjayed udariṇa<cb n="2"/>m virikto yo
                        'bhipūryate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.13"> yonīsamvaraṇaṃ saṅgaḥ kukṣo makkallasaṃjñitaḥ
                        | hanyuḥ striyaṃ mūḍhaga-<lb n="4"/>rvbhe yathoktāś cāpy upadravāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.15"> visaṃjñas tām yate yas tu śete nipati-<cb
                            n="2"/>to yathā | śītārddito 'ntaruṣṇaś ca
                        <caesura/>
                         jvareṇa mriyate naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.16"> yo hṛṣṭaromā raktākṣo hṛdi saṃghātaśūla<lb
                            n="5"/>vān | vaktreṇa cocchvasiti taṃ jvaro hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.17"> hikkāśvāsa samā<cb n="2"/>yuktaṃ mūḍham
                        vibhrāntalocanaṃ | santatocchvāsinaṃ kṣīṇaṃ naraṃ kṣapayate jvaraḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.18">
                        <gap reason="not in manuscript"/></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.19"> śvāsaśūlapipāsārtaṃ-<lb n="7"/>kṣīṇañ
                        jvaranipīḍitaṃ | viśeṣeṇa naraṃ vṛddham atīsāro vināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.20"> śuklākṣamannadveṣṭāram ūrddhaśvāsanipīḍitam |
                        kṛcchreṇa vahu mehantaṃ yakṣmā hantīha mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.21"> śvāsaśūlapipā<pb n="67r"/>sānnavidveṣo
                        granthimūḍhatā | jāyate durvvalatvaṃ ca gulmino maraṇāya vai|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.22"> ādhmānaṃ vaddhaniṣyandaṃ
                        ccharddihikkātṛṣānvitam | rujāśvāsasamāyuktaṃ vidradhir nnāśayet
                        naraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.23"> pāṇḍudantanakho <lb n="2"/>yastu pāṇḍunetraś
                        ca mānavaḥ | pāṇḍusaṃghātadarśī ca pāṇḍurogī vina<lb n="3"/>śyati
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.24"> lohitañ charddayed yas tu vahuśo lohitekṣaṇaḥ
                        | lohito ṅgāradarśī ca mriyate raktapaittikaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.25">
                        <lb n="4"/>avāco pi savāco 'pi kṣīṇamānsavalo naraḥ | jāgarūko
                            <unclear reason="transliteror's lack of expertise"

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.3"><add place="inline">bhavet pāṇi<lb n="3"
                            />talaṃ lehaḥ svarasas tu paladvayaṃ |
                            <caesura/>
                             vyādhyādīnām bale madhye mā<cb/>traiṣā śamanauṣadhai
                        ||</add></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.4"><add place="inline">ato jñātveṣṭato yojyo
                            hīmahī nādhikedhikāḥ |
                            <caesura/>
                             jñātvā koṣṭhauṣadhabalam mātrā<lb n="4"/>kalpyā suśobhane
                            ||</add></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.12">cale doṣe mṛdau koṣṭhe nekṣan tatra balan nṛṇāṃ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                        <lb n="5"/>avyāpadurbbalasyāpi śodhanaṃ hi tadā bhavet</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.13"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.14"/>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti || la<unclear>ḍe</unclear> || || ||</p>
                </div>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.1"> athāto dravyarasavīryavipākavijñānīyam
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.2"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.3"> kecid ācāryā vruvate | <lb n="6"/> dravyam
                        pradhānam kasmāt vyavasthitatvāt | iha khalu dravyam
                        vyavasthitanna rasādayaḥ | yathā <unclear>ye</unclear> phale
                        rasādayas te pakve na bhavanti || nityatvāc ca nityaṃ hi
                        dravyamanityaṃ hi guṇāḥ | yathā ka<pb
                            n="dscn3056fol080_bottom.jpg"/>lkādi pravibhāgās tad eva
                        sampannarasagandhaṃ vyāpannarasagandhavān bhavatīti |
                        svajātivyavasthānāc ca yathā pārthivaṃ dravyam anyabhāvan na
                        gacchati | evaṃ śoṣāṇi | pañcendri<lb n="2"/>yagrahaṇāc ca |
                        pañcaindriyair gṛhyate draṣṭavyanna rasādaya<cb/>ḥ | āśrayatvāc ca
                        dravyam āśritārasā iti | ārambha sāmarthyāc ca dravyāśrita
                        ārambhaḥ || yathā vidārigandhā<lb n="3"/>dim āhṛtyāva<unclear/>dya
                        vipaced ity evam ādiṣu na rasādiṣ ā<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"
                        /><cb/>rambhaḥ | śāstraprāmāṇyāc ca śāstraṃ <unclear/>ha |
                        dvividhan dravyaṃ sthāvarañjañgam<unclear/>ti | kramāpekṣikatvāc
                        ca rasā<lb n="4"/>dīnāṃ rasādayo hi dravyakramam apekṣante yathā
                        taruṇe ta<cb/>ruṇāḥ | saṃpūrṇa sampūrṇā iti | ekadeśasādhyatvāc ca
                        dravyāṇām ekadeśenāpi vyādhayaḥ sādhyante | yathā<lb n="5"/>
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇeti | tasmād dravyam pradhānan rasādaya<cb/>ḥ
                        kasmāt niravayavatvāt dravyasya | dravyalakṣaṇan tu
                        kriyāguṇasamavāyaḥ kriyādravye vidyate | guṇāḥ sa<lb n="6"
                        />mavāyakāraṇañceti ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.4"> netyāhur anye rasās tu pradhānan kasmāt āgamāt
                        āgamo hi śāstram ity ucyate | <pb n="dscn3057fol081_top.jpg"
                        />śāstre rasā adhikṛtā yathā rasāyatta āhāra iti | upadeśāc ca |
                        upadiśyate hi | yathā madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaṃ śamayanti | <lb n="2"
                        /> ato rasāḥ pradhānaṃ | anumāc ca | rasato hy anumīyate
                        dra<cb/>vyaṃ | yathā madhuram iti || ṛṣivacanāc ca | ṛṣivacano
                        vedaḥ | yathā kiñcidījyārtham madhuramāhared iti<lb n="3"/> |
                        tasmāt rasāḥ pradhānaṃ | raseṣu tu guṇasaṃjñā rasalakṣaṇa<cb/>m
                        atro padekṣyāmaḥ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.5"> netyāhur anye vīryam pradhānam iti | kasmāt
                        prādhānyāt | ihatvauṣadhakarmmāṇi vīrya prādhā<lb n="4"/>nyaṃ na
                        bhavanti | tad yathā |
                        urddhabhāgodhobhāgobhayabhāgasaṃ<cb/>śamanaṃ
                        sāṅgrāhikadīpanalekhanavṛṃhaṇarasāyanavājīkaraṇaś ca
                            yathuharavilayanadāraṇamarddana<lb n="5"
                        />prāṇaghnaviṣapraśamanāni vīrya prādhānyena bhavanti | tantu<cb/>

                        aṣṭavidham āhuḥ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ snigdhaṃ rūkṣam vi<lb n="6"/> ṣadam
                        piccilam mṛdus tīkṣṇañ ceti | etāni khalu vīryāṇi

                        tāvad vṛhatyañ ca mūlaṅ kaṣāya tiktaṃ vātaṃ śamayaty uṣṇavīrya<pb
                            n="dscn3057fol081_bottom.jpg"/>tvāt | kaṭukā pippalīpittaṃ
                        śamayati | mṛduśītavīryatvāt | tiktā kākamācī pittaṃ varddhayaty
                        uṣṇavīryatvāt | kaṭukaṃ mūlaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ varddhayati
                        snigdhavīryatvāt | amlaṃ kapitthaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ <lb n="2"
                        /><unclear/>ti rukṣavīryatvāt || <unclear>bha</unclear> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.6"> ye rasā vātaśamanā bhavanti <cb/> yadi teṣu vai
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         rukṣalāghavaśaity āni na te hanyuḥ samīraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.7"> ye rasāḥ pittaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu<g
                            ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="3"/>vai |

                         taikṣṇyauṣṇyalaghutā caiva na te talkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.8"> ye rasāḥ śleṣma<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"
                        /><cb/>śamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehagauravaśaity ānu na te tatkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.9"> tasmād vīryaṃ pradhānam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.10">
                        <lb n="4"/>netyāhur anye vipākaḥ pradhānam iti | kasmāt samyaṅ
                        mithyā vipa<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>kvatvāt | iha hi
                        dravyāṇyapaha tāni samyaṅ mithyā cāvipakvāni guṇan doṣam vā
                        janayaṃti | tatrāhur anye prati ra<lb n="5"/> sampāka iti |
                        vipākaḥ kecit trividham icchanti | madhuram amlam kaṭuka<cb/>ñceti
                        | tat tu na samyak | bhūtaguṇādāgamāc cāmlo vipāko nāsti | pittaṃ
                        hi vidagdham amlatām upaity āgneyatvāt | <lb n="6"/> yad evaṃ
                        lavaṇo 'pyanyaḥ pāke bhaviṣyati | śleṣmā hi vidagdho lavaṇatām
                        upaiti | tamādasiddhānta eṣaḥ | pratirasam amlāmlasyaivaṃ
                        sarvvaṣām iti dṛṣṭāntañ codāharanti | yathā śāliyava<pb
                            n="dscn3058fol082_top.jpg"/>mudgādayaḥ prakīrṇāḥ svabhāvam
                        uttarakāle pi na parity ajanti tadvat iti | kecit punar avalavanto
                        valavatāṃ vaśamāyānt it evam avasthitaḥ pāka iti | āgame svāha |
                        dvividha eva pāko madhuraḥ kaṭukaś ca <lb n="2"/> | tayor
                        madhurākhyo guruḥ kaṭukākhyo laghur iti | tatra
                        pṛthivyaptejovā<cb/>yvākāśānāṃ dvaividhyam bhavati |
                        guṇasādharmyāngurutā | laghutā ca pṛthivyā yo gurvyaḥ | śeṣāṇi
                        laghūni tasmād dvivi<lb n="3"/>dha eva pāko bhavati || bha ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.11"> dravyeṣu pacyamāneṣu yeṣv amvupṛthi<g
                            ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>vīguṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivarttante 'dhikās tatra pāko madhura ucyate || </l>

                        <caesura/>
                         niva<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="4"/>rttante 'dhikās tatra
                        pākaḥ kaṭuka ucyate || </l>

                        vādasaṃgrahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                            n="5"/> sevitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         āgamenopayojyāni bheṣajāni vica<lb n="2"/>kṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

                        <caesura/>

                <div n="42" type="adhyāya">
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.1"> athāto rasaviśeṣavi-<cb n="2"/>jñānīyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.2"> </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.3"> ākāśapavanadahanatoyabhūmiṣu yathāsaṅkhyam

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519">daśaivādyām pravakṣyāmi dravādīstām̐<cb/>ś
                        chṛṇuśva me ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.514">śītaḥ prahlādanastambhī mūrcchātṛṭsvedadāhajit
                        ||1||
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇastad viparītaḥ syāt pāca<lb n="5"/>naś ca viśeṣataḥ ||2||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.515">sneho mārddavakṛt snigdho valavarṇṇa<cb/>karas
                        tathā ||3||
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣas tad viparītaḥ syād viśeṣāt stambhanaḥ smṛtaḥ ||4||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.516">picchilo jīvanaśle<lb n="6"/>ṣī sandhāno
                        vṛṃhaṇas tathā ||5||
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣado viparīto 'sya bhedī śodhanaropaṇaḥ ||6||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.517">dāhapākakaras tīkṣṇaḥ śrāvaṇo mṛduranyathā
                        ||8||
                        <caesura/>
                         sāndropalepaḥ kaphakṛ<pb n="123v"/>d guruḥ prīṇanavṛṃhaṇaḥ
                        ||10||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.518ab">laghus tad viparītaḥ syāl lekhano ropaṇas
                        tathā ||11||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519cd">dravaḥ prakledanaḥ sāndraḥ śuṣkaḥ syād
                        dvandvakārakaḥ ||13||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519ef">ślakṣṇaḥ picchilava jñeyaḥ ka<lb n="2"
                        />rkkaśo viṣado yathā ||15||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.520">sukhānuvarttī sūkṣmañ ca sugandhī<cb/>rocano
                        mataḥ ||15||
                        <caesura/>
                         durggandho viparīto sya prakāśau cāpy ubhāv api ||17||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.521">saro 'nulomanaḥ<lb n="3"/> prokto mando
                        yātrākaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||19||
                        <caesura/>
                         vyavāyī deham akhilaṃ<cb/> vyāpya pākāya kalpate ||20||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.522"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.523">guṇā viṃśatir ity ete karmmataḥ parikīrttitāḥ
                            ||<unclear unit="syllable"/></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.524">ata ūrddham pravakṣyāmi āhāragatiniścayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcabhūtātmake de<cb/>he āhāraḥ pākabhautikaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vipakvaḥ pañcadhā samyag guṇām̐s tān abhivarddhayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.525">avidagdhaṃ kaphaṃ pittam vidagdhaḥ pavanam
                        punaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         samyag vipakṣo niḥsāra āhāraḥ<cb/> parivṛṃhayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.526">viṇmūtram āhāramalaḥ sāraḥ prāgīrito rasaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sa tu vyānena vikṣiptaḥ sarvvān dhā<lb n="6"/>tūn visarppati
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.527">kaphapittamalaḥ kheṣu svedaḥ syān nakharoma ca
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         netraviṭ tvakṣu ca sneho dhātūnāṃ kramaśo malāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.528">divāvivuddhahṛdaye jāgrataḥ puṇḍarīkavat ||
                        <caesura/>
                         anupakli<pb n="124r"/>nna dhātvannam ajīrṇṇepi hitaṃ niśi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.529">hṛdayaṃ līyate rātrau prasuptasya viśeṣataḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         samupaklinnadhātvannam ajīrṇṇe tvahitaṃ divā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.530">imam vidhiṃ yo 'numatam mahāmuner
                            mmaharṣimu<lb n="2"/>khyasya paṭhet tu yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa bhūmipāloya vidhātum auṣadham mahā<cb/>tmanāñ cārhati
                        vaidyasattama iti || o ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.531"><add place="inline">dravyajñānaṃ rasajñānam
                            vasanañ ca virecanaṃ |
                            <caesura/>
                             dravadravya<lb n="3"/>parijñānam annapānena ṣaṭ smṛtaḥ || o
                            ||</add></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.532"><add place="inline">sūtrasthāne purā<cb/>
                            proktañ catvāriṃśat ṣaḍuttaraṃ |
                            <caesura/>
                             adhyāyāḥ kāśirājena pūrṇṇaṃ sarvvaṃ savistaraṃ ||</add></l>

                    <p ana="trailer">|| iti<lb n="4"/>suśrute śalyatantre sūtrasthānaṃ
                        samāptaṃ || ||</p>
